        network 500 create
            description "for marking"
            ingress
                default-action fc be profile in
                dscp be fc be profile in
                dscp cs1 fc l2 profile in
                dscp cs2 fc l2 profile in
                dscp cs3 fc l2 profile in
                dscp cs4 fc h1 profile in
                dscp cs5 fc af profile in
                dscp nc1 fc nc profile in
                dscp nc2 fc af profile in
                lsp-exp 0 fc be profile in
                lsp-exp 1 fc l2 profile in
                lsp-exp 2 fc l2 profile in
                lsp-exp 3 fc l2 profile in
                lsp-exp 4 fc h1 profile in
                lsp-exp 5 fc af profile in
                lsp-exp 6 fc nc profile in
                lsp-exp 7 fc af profile in
            exit
            egress
                remarking
                fc af
                    dscp-in-profile cs5
                    dscp-out-profile cs5
                    lsp-exp-in-profile 5
                    lsp-exp-out-profile 5
                exit
                fc h1
                    dscp-in-profile cs4
                    dscp-out-profile cs4
                    lsp-exp-in-profile 4
                    lsp-exp-out-profile 4
                exit
                fc nc
                    dscp-in-profile nc1
                    dscp-out-profile nc1
                    lsp-exp-in-profile 6
                    lsp-exp-out-profile 6
                exit
            exit
        exit
    exit
